<DESCRIPTION>REVENUE AND EARNINGS EXPECTATIONS UPDATE
<TEXT>
<html><head>
<!-- Document created using Wdesk -->
<!-- Copyright 2024 Workiva -->
<title>Document</title></head><body><div id="ia397037ae9ab432e90209693227ce767_1"></div><div style="min-height:99pt;width:100%"><div style="text-align:right"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:right"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Exhibit 99.1</font></div><div style="text-align:right"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><img alt="luluwordmarka.jpg" src="luluwordmarka.jpg" style="height:36px;margin-bottom:5pt;vertical-align:text-bottom;width:186px"></div></div><div style="margin-top:14pt;text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:115%">lululemon athletica inc. Updates Revenue and Earnings Expectations </font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:115%">for the Fourth Quarter Ahead of the ICR Conference</font></div><div style="margin-top:5pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Vancouver, British Columbia &#8211; January 8, 2024</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> &#8211; lululemon athletica inc. (NASDAQ&#58;LULU) today announced that, for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2023, the Company now expects net revenue will be in the range of $3.170 billion to $3.190 billion, representing a 14% to 15% increase compared to the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022. The previous guidance range was $3.135 billion to $3.170 billion. </font></div><div style="margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Diluted earnings per share are now expected to be in the range of $4.96 to $5.00 for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2023 compared to the Company&#8217;s previous guidance range of $4.85 to $4.93.</font></div><div style="margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The Company now expects gross margin to be in the range of 58.6% to 58.7% for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2023, compared to its previous guidance of 58.3% to 58.6%. There is no change to the Company&#8217;s previous guidance for selling, general, and administrative expenses or effective tax rate.</font></div><div style="margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Meghan Frank, Chief Financial Officer, commented&#58; &#8220;We are pleased with our performance during the holiday season, as guests continue to respond well to our innovative and versatile product offerings. Our sales trend remains balanced across channels, categories, and geographies, enabling us to raise our guidance for the fourth quarter and close out another strong year.&#8221;</font></div><div style="margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Management will be meeting with analysts and investors at the ICR Conference on January 8-10, 2024.</font></div><div id="ia397037ae9ab432e90209693227ce767_59"></div><div style="margin-top:14pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">About lululemon athletica inc.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">lululemon athletica inc. (NASDAQ&#58;LULU) is a technical athletic apparel, footwear, and accessories company for yoga, running, training, and most other activities, creating transformational products and experiences that build meaningful connections, unlocking greater possibility and wellbeing for all.&#160;Setting the bar in innovation of fabrics and functional designs, lululemon works with yogis and athletes in local communities around the world for continuous research and product feedback.&#160;For more information, visit lululemon.com.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:14pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Forward-Looking Statements&#58; </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">This press release includes estimates, projections, statements relating to the Company's business plans, objectives, and expected operating results that are &#34;forward-looking statements&#34; within the meaning of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995, Section 27A of the Securities Act of 1933 and Section 21E of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934. if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
